, &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Others were buried up to their necks and were\nthen run over by battle tanks. Chinese would be herded in large groups, sprayed\nwith gasoline and set on fire. Infants were dropped into boiling water. Young\nboys were sliced in half with swords.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oce2QtBSNeM/UH69Rvw4JaI/AAAAAAAAVUA/VCqyMDnWygs/s1600/article-2205870-0024CAEE00000258-744_634x622.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"626\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oce2QtBSNeM/UH69Rvw4JaI/AAAAAAAAVUA/VCqyMDnWygs/s320/article-2205870-0024CAEE00000258-744_634x622.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Vicious dogs were set loose on Chinese and ripped them\napart whilst crowds of Japanese enjoyed the spectacle, like in the old days of\ngladiator Rome.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">They would chop off the\n4 limbs just to record how long the body will twitch.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">This would be repeated for various ages and\nfor men, women and children.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">These were NOT\nscientific experiments under any figment of human imagination- it was just for\nthe sadistic pleasure of seeing the people suffer.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">All these records are still there in the US lab at Maryland. &nbsp;Hey, was it printed on the US dollar IN GOD WE TRUST?</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Chinese were thrown into the icy river where they would\ninstantly be frozen solid whereupon their bodies would be riddled with machine\ngun bullets &nbsp;There are many photographs which\nshow Japanese soldiers beheading captives or conducting bayonet practice upon\nthem with a smile , as laughing Japanese soldiers in the background clapped. &nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">It was believed by many Japanese that eating\nthe penises of their fallen enemy would increase their virility. . They sliced\nbabies in half or even in quarters with their bayonets, while the parents\nwatched in horror. &nbsp;The Japanese soldiers\nforced fathers to rape their daughters, while they watched like a live blue\nmovie. &nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jwwKd5Mal9U/UH7PycxiFfI/AAAAAAAAVYc/syAtFbeYuoE/s1600/imagesmnbgfeee.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"321\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jwwKd5Mal9U/UH7PycxiFfI/AAAAAAAAVYc/syAtFbeYuoE/s1600/imagesmnbgfeee.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Nanking became a city of complete\nsavagery. &nbsp;Anyone caught in the streets\nby the soldiers faced beheading at the hands of the Japanese samurai sword. &nbsp;They took pride in slicing them in one\nblow.&nbsp; Japanese soldiers had a sport competition\ngoing, to see who could kill the most Chinese, in the fastest manner\u2014and these\nwere timed and recorded on paper or photographs. &nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">\n</span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-KhowJ7SBKRk/UH693rND4oI/AAAAAAAAVUY/2-QI24J14lk/s1600/imageshllmng.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-KhowJ7SBKRk/UH693rND4oI/AAAAAAAAVUY/2-QI24J14lk/s1600/imageshllmng.jpg\" width=\"448\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The Japanese soldiers kept a &nbsp;score with decapitated heads, in the\nbeginning. Later, they simply slit throats.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">According to Japanese Lieutenant colonel\nToshio Ohta's statement, between December 14 and December 18 alone, QUOTE: the\nJapanese commanding headquarters of Nanjing Port disposed of 100,000 bodies\nwhile other troops disposed of 50,000. UNQUOTE .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In 1937, the Osaka\nMainichi Shimbun and its sister newspaper the Tokyo Nichi Nichi Shimbun covered\na \"contest\" between two Japanese officers, Toshiaki Mukai &nbsp;and Tsuyoshi Noda , in which the two men were\ndescribed as vying with one another to be the first to kill 100 people with a\nsword.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Young girls would be\nliterally raped to death, their bodies mutilated by swords or bayonets into\ntheir vaginas afterwards. &nbsp;If you check\nout the vaginal wound, you could make out if it was done by an officer with a\nsword or a soldier with a bayonet. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jllT6u-IGgQ/UH7NtIH0RlI/AAAAAAAAVW0/UnbsJ821J08/s1600/imageskkmbrgt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"223\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jllT6u-IGgQ/UH7NtIH0RlI/AAAAAAAAVW0/UnbsJ821J08/s320/imageskkmbrgt.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The women raped as much\nas 40 times a day &nbsp;would be unable to\nwalk \u2013they just lay there with their legs open. &nbsp;Many survivors later died of their wounds or\ndisease. Women would be tied down onto furniture with their legs spread on the\nsidewalks of the street and would be successively raped by countless soldiers\nwho happened to pass by. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Japanese soldiers took\nmany photographs for keepsakes and souvenirs of the women that were raped and\nmutilated. There are photos of dead women with rods shoved into their vaginas.\nEyewitness and photographs described whole streets and alleys full of such victims. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ZQ-pkWTOO2o/UH7ODuRF3bI/AAAAAAAAVXE/NT2Iqy9VmIE/s1600/imagesgghjkktfvbb.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"295\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ZQ-pkWTOO2o/UH7ODuRF3bI/AAAAAAAAVXE/NT2Iqy9VmIE/s1600/imagesgghjkktfvbb.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">As in the case of the\nmass execution of the Chinese males, Japanese soldiers invented raping games\nand contest. Brothers were forced to rape their sisters and sons were forced to\nrape their mothers. Fathers were forced to rape their daughters. Anyone\nrefusing to participate would be executed on the spot.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Young female virgins\nwere especially prized by the Japanese. As in the case of the eating of\npenises, many Japanese soldiers actually cut out the vaginas of young girls and\nfashioned keepsakes made out of the victims pubic hair. It was believed by many\nJapanese soldiers that the pubic hair of a virgin would make them invulnerable\nto enemy fire.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Q8XP8k3bvRo/UH64xCF4rKI/AAAAAAAAVSI/Xy2NHO85pzY/s1600/imageshgjiopo.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"280\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Q8XP8k3bvRo/UH64xCF4rKI/AAAAAAAAVSI/Xy2NHO85pzY/s1600/imageshgjiopo.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">As early as 1932, the\nJapanese government established a system of&nbsp;\nmilitary sexual slavery, the so-called \u201ccomfort-stations\u201d where\nthousands of&nbsp; women, particularly from\nKorea, China, Japan, and the Philippines, but also women throughout Asia, were\ntricked or forced into prostitution and used as sex slaves by the Japanese\nsoldiers. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">There were more than\n2000 of such comfort stations. Recently I saw a \u201ccomfort station\u201d in an Indian\nrailway station. This was a&nbsp; toilet. I\nguess nobody heard the concept of military whorehouses in India.</span> &nbsp;<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The Japanese soldiers referred to\nthese military whorehouses as \u201cpublic toilets\u201d and treated them as such.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vsDhCnWpx4Y/UH63z4OfBjI/AAAAAAAAVRg/9SkMwUAjxUQ/s1600/imageshjkioih.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"272\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vsDhCnWpx4Y/UH63z4OfBjI/AAAAAAAAVRg/9SkMwUAjxUQ/s1600/imageshjkioih.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">These poor women were\nsubjected to constant degradation, verbal and physical abuse. &nbsp;Some were girls as young as twelve years old\u2014and\nsome of these girls still live. &nbsp;The\nprettiest and the youngest girls were reserved for the high ranking officers. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Y0R6WZs1lGo/UH64eWqg1tI/AAAAAAAAVSA/uZOCeubTAQA/s1600/imagesnjjtt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Y0R6WZs1lGo/UH64eWqg1tI/AAAAAAAAVSA/uZOCeubTAQA/s400/imagesnjjtt.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Every attractive girl\nof 12 year and more , were kidnapped and sent them to officially sanctioned\nmilitary brothels. </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The more attractive\nones would be raped more. They would</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">face\nbeatings and physical pain if they did NOT obey unnatural and perverted orders\n.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">This form of&nbsp; abuse during war has come to be known as the\n\u201chidden horror\u201d because women who suffered this kind of &nbsp;abuse have endured in silence even after the\nwar because of&nbsp; their shame and\nhumiliation.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Dr. Ishii dehumanized\nhis victims, designating them as muralas or \u201clogs,\u201d a sick joke that originated\nwhen the Japanese told the local Manchurians that Unit 731 facility was being\nbuilt as \u201ca lumber mill.\u201d <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-J7NjJaKdj-U/UH7OraYiUfI/AAAAAAAAVXk/zPaIi4bCQ-M/s1600/imagesuyf,mhjf.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-J7NjJaKdj-U/UH7OraYiUfI/AAAAAAAAVXk/zPaIi4bCQ-M/s400/imagesuyf,mhjf.jpg\" width=\"484\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Unit 731 was 6 square\nkilometres in size. &nbsp;Maps show 76\ndifferent structures , laboratories, dissection rooms, barns for experimental\nanimals, dormitories for the 20,000 staff - serviced by its own airport and\nrailway spur. &nbsp;The staff included&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">physicians, surgeons,\nnurses, chemists, biologists, microbiologists, veterinarians, entomologists,\nand plant pathologists.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">These scientists and medical personnel were paid extra\nfor their work. Surprisingly, although the development of</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">CBW and the medical experiments were done in\nsecret, the Japanese medical community was well-informed about these\nexperiments. In fact, several \ufb01lms of</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;\n</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">the vivisections were shown in Japan.</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">It housed administrative\nbuildings, laboratories, workers dormitories, barracks, an autopsy-dissecting\nbuilding and a special prison to house human test subjects.&nbsp; Three giant furnaces handled \u201cdisposal\u201d of human\ncarcasses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The rationale behind\nconducting a vivisection upon a living subject previously infected with a germ\nwarfare agent was to observe the damage wrought on the victim's internal organs\nwhilst the victim WAS STILL ALIVE.&nbsp; It\nwas felt that utilizing a general anesthetic upon the victims thus\n\"treated\" may inhibit the progress of the germ warfare agent.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">There are photographs\nof \u201cdoctor death\u201d Shiro Ishii, in his general's uniform, &nbsp;proudly bearing on his breast the Golden Kite\n(Third Order) and Rising Sun (Middle Chord) medals personally presented to him\nby Hirohito . The atrocities were committed by some of Japan's most\ndistinguished doctors recruited by Dr. Ishii. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yUYHRhai4C0/UH63fjn_eVI/AAAAAAAAVRQ/v-kVSdB4zdQ/s1600/shiro_ishii_1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-yUYHRhai4C0/UH63fjn_eVI/AAAAAAAAVRQ/v-kVSdB4zdQ/s320/shiro_ishii_1.jpg\" width=\"448\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Many of Ishii's\nexperiments can only be described as psychopathically sadistic, with no\nconceivable military application. But the weapon was so uncontrollable that\nIshii managed to kill several thousand of his own troops. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">No fewer than 700 of\nthe doctors responsible for these ghastly experiments received the highest\nhonours for scientific achievement, publishing more than 100 papers in which\nthey disguised the true nature of their experiments by referring to \u201cChinese\nmonkeys\" . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The Chinese were\ninfected with plague, anthrax, cholera, and other pathogens.&nbsp; They were subjected to experiments to study\nthe effects of&nbsp; frostbite, dehydration,\nand malnutrition as well as experimental surgeries in transplantation of&nbsp; limbs from one individual to another. Neither\nwomen nor children were spared.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Women were subjected to\nsimilar medical experiments as men. The women were subjected to forced\nparticipation in studies of&nbsp;\nsexually-transmitted diseases (STDs).&nbsp;\nAt&nbsp; \ufb01rst syphilis was injected.\nThen the Japanese decided they could study the effects better if&nbsp; the syphilis was contracted through sexual\ncontact: they forced women to have sex with men who were infected.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zeZRNs0zXv8/UH7MexLkqSI/AAAAAAAAVWE/K3Wxs7Udnr8/s1600/tumblr_lys9e4VYUx1r15w5uo2_250.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"486\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zeZRNs0zXv8/UH7MexLkqSI/AAAAAAAAVWE/K3Wxs7Udnr8/s400/tumblr_lys9e4VYUx1r15w5uo2_250.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The progress of&nbsp; the disease was closely observed, and women\nwere subjected to live dissection of their internal organs to investigate the\ndifferent stages of&nbsp; the syphilis . Experiments\nwere conducted on babies born in Unit 731 as well as on children brought to the\nunit. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Some prisoners had\ntheir stomachs surgically removed and the esophagus reattached to the\nintestines. &nbsp;Parts of the brain, lungs,\nliver, etc. were removed from some prisoners . Prisoners were infested with\nfleas in order to acquire large quantities of disease-carrying fleas for the\npurposes of studying the viability of germ warfare.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span></span><br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span></span>\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Babies were subjected\nto experimentation and dissection.&nbsp;\nChildren as young as 6 years were used in germ and chemical tests. These\nso-called \u201clogs\u201d were not meant to survive.&nbsp;\nOnce a prisoner was sent to a biological warfare (BW) facility, the\nsystem mandated that the person would not live.&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span></span>\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span></span>\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Most lasted only 30 days.&nbsp; They were infected, dissected without\nanesthesia, usually a vivisection, dispatched by lethal injection, and then\ncremated in an on-site crematorium.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qXa80AukTJM/UH7XK4Z8NaI/AAAAAAAAVa8/NVYB44BiT5k/s1600/imagesrurjrnxb.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"311\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qXa80AukTJM/UH7XK4Z8NaI/AAAAAAAAVa8/NVYB44BiT5k/s400/imagesrurjrnxb.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Other incidents include\nbeing deprived of food and water to determine the length of time until death,\nbeing placed into high-pressure chambers until death, having experiments\nperformed upon prisoners to determine the relationship between temperature,\nburns, and human survival, being placed into centrifuges and spun until dead.&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Human subjects were\nplaced in pressure chambers to see how much pressure they could withstand\nbefore their eyeballs popped out of their skulls.</span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The Japanese injected animal blood and studied the effects.. Chinese were exposed to lethal\ndoses of x-rays. Various chemical weapons tested on prisoners inside gas\nchambers. Chinese were injected with sea water in various concentrations to determine if it could be a substitute\nfor saline.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-VUqemHOGqaE/UH7OMrNcQ3I/AAAAAAAAVXM/MUAnTzHFkxo/s1600/imageskkkuytrv.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"362\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-VUqemHOGqaE/UH7OMrNcQ3I/AAAAAAAAVXM/MUAnTzHFkxo/s400/imageskkkuytrv.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n\n</span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Chinese were buried\nalive to check out if they could go into hibernation with selected chemicals .\nSome were subjected to sub-freezing temperatures.&nbsp; Later they were \u201cdefrosted\u201d by a range of\nexperimental techniques.&nbsp; It was usual\nfor these \u201clogs\u201d to have their limbs beaten with sticks until they resounded\nwith a hard, hollow ring - signifying the freezing process was complete<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Humans were used in\nfrostbite experiments and burned with flamethrowers to determine means to treat\nJapanese soldiers thus wounded.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Victims were bombarded\nwith lethal doses of X-Rays. Even newborn infants were used in these ghastly\nexperiments.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Vivisection of living\npeople (including pregnant women who were impregnated by the doctors),\nprisoners had limbs amputated and reattached to other parts of their body, some\nprisoners had parts of their bodies frozen and thawed to study the resulting\nuntreated gangrene. Humans were also used as living test cases for grenades and\nflame throwers. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Prisoners were injected\nwith inoculations of disease, disguised as vaccinations, to study their effects.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">To study the effects of\nuntreated venereal diseases, male and female prisoners were deliberately\ninfected with syphilis and gonorrhea via rape, then studied.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">'Body without organs'\nevisceration initiative was undertaken, alongside other unprecedented explorations\ninto the extreme zones of the human body and its sensations.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Chinese were infected\nwith Bubonic Plague and other Biowarfare toxins such as Anthrax, Syphilis,\nTyphus and a variety of other biowarfare agents. Victims infected with germ\nwarfare agents were placed in confinement with healthy subjects to see how long\nit would take for the healthy subjects to become infected and die. Chinese were\nthe human guinea pigs in all these horrific experiments.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Plague-infested fleas,\nbred in the laboratories of Unit 731 and Unit 1644, were spread by low-flying\nairplanes upon Chinese cities, coastal Ningbo in 1940, and Changde, Hunan\nProvince, in 1941. This military aerial spraying killed thousands of people\nwith bubonic plague epidemics.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The Japanese Army dropped\ncholera and typhoid cultures in wells and ponds in various parts of China. &nbsp;Poison Gas attacks were used on the Chinese.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Pingfan had 4,500 flea\nbreeding machines which produced 100 million infected fleas every few days.\nThese fleas, infected with plague, typhoid, cholera and anthrax organisms, were\nto be dropped on invaded countries to inherit the land without a human\npopulation.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Subjects were tied to\nboards and shielded with metal sheets while a bomb outfitted with the plague or\nanthrax was exploded before them, then monitored for days as they succumbed to\nthe viruses. Their limbs were frozen and amputated to test hypothermia, blood\nloss and fighting capacity.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">There were pens where squirrels\nwere bred, a cool room where prisoners were taken to have their limbs frozen, and a boiler room to thaw. Plague and cholera were the two most\npromising germs. But almost anything else that could kill was tried at one time\nor another - anthrax, typhoid, dysentery, tuberculosis, syphilis, salmonella,\ntetanus, gas gangrene, meningitis, yellow fever, glanders (a horse disease), as\nwell as electrocution, freezing to death, fugu fish poison, injections of air,\nphosgene gas and potassium cyanide&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">One documents the time taken to freeze to\ndeath three-day-old babies. In another, a man had his leg amputated and his arm\nsewn on in its place. The blood of horses was injected into people's\nkidneys.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The scale of Ishii's diabolical ambitions was huge. Enough germs were\nbrewed up here to kill everyone on earth many times over; at full capacity, 300\nkilos of plague bacteria were produced every month, 500 kilos of anthrax, and\nnearly a tonne of dysentery and cholera. At Anda airfield, 150 kilometres north\nof Harbin, scores of prisoners were tied to stakes in a field while the\nJapanese Air Force bombarded them with explosive shells, cluster-bombs and\naerosols of deadly diseases.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Rats carrying fleas\ninfected with plague were released into the countryside. One record that\nsurvived the bonfire shows that Ishii wanted to transport these rats by midget\nsubmarine to be released in the streets of invaded countries.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Ishii gave children\nchocolates laced with anthrax, biscuits laden with plague; he fed prisoners of\nwar typhoid-infected dumplings, and tea, coffee and beer laced with other\npathogens.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Ishii's men infecting\nhundreds of wells and reservoirs, and scattering germ-dosed wheat and millet\naround. Within weeks, thousands had died and the town was ravaged by plague,\ncholera and typhoid for the next seven years.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">A documentary film made about\nthis \"success\" was shown to appreciative audiences of scientists and\nmilitary personnel back in Japan. &nbsp;Jing\nFuhe, then a boy of 10, recalls watching in amazement as an extraordinary\nmenagerie of sick animals escaped from the ruins of the death factory - camels,\nmonkeys, rats, bears, squirrels, horses. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On August 20, Unit 731 let loose sixty horses\nthat had been fed with glanders-infected oats.&nbsp;\nThese radiated out in different directions tovillages, where they\ninfected other animals.&nbsp; On that same\nday, Unit 731 set free thousands of&nbsp;\nbubonic plague infected rats.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\nNo less a witness than Prince Takahito, brother of Emperor Hirohito, confessed in an interview earlier this year that he had seen poison gas experiments and bayonet practice on prisoners.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">After Japan\u2019s surrender\non August 15, 1945, this facility outside the city of Harbin was set on \ufb01re.&nbsp; The remaining prisoners are gassed.&nbsp; A mass grave is dug. Furthermore, the works of Yoshiaki Yoshimi and Seiya Matsuno show that\nthe Emperor authorized, by specific orders (rinsanmei), the use of chemical\nweapons against the Chinese.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BX5WsqpTz3Y/UH7Qq9ofPyI/AAAAAAAAVZU/Jmf4jH0UdfE/s1600/imagesjjkiooo.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"404\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BX5WsqpTz3Y/UH7Qq9ofPyI/AAAAAAAAVZU/Jmf4jH0UdfE/s400/imagesjjkiooo.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Many historians see\nEmperor Hirohito as responsible for the atrocities committed by the imperial\nforces in the Second Sino-Japanese War and in World War II and feel that he,\nsome members of the imperial family such as his brother Prince Chichibu, his\ncousins Prince Takeda and Prince Fushimi, and his uncles Prince Kan'in, Prince\nAsaka, and Prince Higashikuni, should have been tried for war crimes.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In Japan, debate over the Emperor's\nresponsibility was taboo while he was still alive. After his death, 7th Jan\n1989 however, debate began to surface over the extent of his involvement and\nthus his culpability.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-daX46uGLOPk/UH7PnzMhGNI/AAAAAAAAVYU/Ml81JIzTOlo/s1600/imageshjjouttgbn.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-daX46uGLOPk/UH7PnzMhGNI/AAAAAAAAVYU/Ml81JIzTOlo/s400/imageshjjouttgbn.jpg\" width=\"301\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">According to the\nJapanese constitution of 1889, the Emperor had a divine power over his country,\nwhich was derived from the shinto belief that the Japanese Imperial Family was\nthe offspring of the sun goddess Amaterasu. Hirohito was however persistent in\nthe idea that the emperor of Japan should be considered a descendant of the\ngods\u2014but he let when when he realized that god or no god, he would be hung,\nlike an ordinary criminal. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In any case, the \"renunciation of\ndivinity\" by Emperor Hirohito, was noted more by foreigners than by\nJapanese, and seems to have been intended for the consumption of the former.The whole idea was USA would get all the biowarfare information without doing it themselves.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The Shinto religion\nencouraged emperor worship, racism, and military aggression Shinto held the\nemperor to be divine&nbsp; because he was\ndeemed to be a descendent of the sun goddess Amaterasu. This&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; provided justification for requiring the\nemperor to be worshipped and obeyed.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\nThe second tenet held that Japan was not just a populated geographical\nfeature &nbsp;in the Pacific Ocean, but a\nland and people created by the sun goddess, and&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; accordingly, specially favoured by the\nancient gods. Finally, Japan was possessed&nbsp;\nof a divine mission to extend its rule and enlightenment to less\nfortunate races. Two atomic blasts paid put their ambitions.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">For the imperial\nJapanese military, bushido meant dedication of their&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; lives to the emperor; defeat was viewed as\nshameful; surrender was dishonourable;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\nthose who surrendered were worthy only of contempt; and compassion for\ndefeated&nbsp; enemies, male or female, the\nelderly, or tiny children, was weakness. The last&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; view was definitely not part of the\ntraditional samurai code of bushido. This&nbsp;perversion of bushido was used to justify countless instances of rape,\nand the&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; murder of prisoners of war,\nwomen, and even tiny children, in countries conquered&nbsp; by the Imperial Japanese military.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; This is the meaning of Shinto nationalism, and the root cause of the Japanese warped mindset and split personalities.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Nationalism in Japan\nhas its root in Shinto or Shintoism. Every child in Japan is taught from\ninfancy to glorify his national traditions in Shinto. The source of Japanese\nShinto mythology is from two sacred books of Japan -- the Kojiki, or Record of\nAncient Matters, and the Nihongi (also known as Nihon Shoki), or Chronicles of\nJapan. These are the two sacred books of Japanese religion, patriotism, and\nimperialism. They provide a moral and ideological background for leaders as\nwell as subjects to draw inspiration and vision to fulfill their destiny.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bTrjghZIRTo/UH7XQ2SnTzI/AAAAAAAAVbE/MS_aamez3LE/s1600/imagesh7i8o.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bTrjghZIRTo/UH7XQ2SnTzI/AAAAAAAAVbE/MS_aamez3LE/s400/imagesh7i8o.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">What makes the Jap\nEmperor\u2019s subjects commit a stylized, stomach splitting hara-kiri in honour of\nhim and to fulfill their collective personal duty?&nbsp; The Emperor, as chief of a contemporary\nstate, is also the high priest in the Shinto religion. Shintoism is the native\nreligion of Japan, primarily a system of nature and ancestor worship which is\ndifficult to understand in our modern society of high technology and industrial\nefficiency.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Yet, millions of Japanese continue to visit an estimated 80,000\nShinto shrines throughout Japan -- where they regularly perform rituals that\ndate back to the dawn of civilized history. Thirteen times a year the Emperor\nof Japan officiates as high priest at major Shinto religious observances.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-z1063h9N8ws/UH68vl5tYJI/AAAAAAAAVTo/oKNQB6j7DGs/s1600/165px-Naiku_01.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-z1063h9N8ws/UH68vl5tYJI/AAAAAAAAVTo/oKNQB6j7DGs/s400/165px-Naiku_01.JPG\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">A\ntypical worship shows the Emperor advancing to the altar, where he offers the\nwine and the rice to the gods. Then he recites a prayer of thanksgiving. The\nEmperor is claimed to have boundless power and this unlimited power is supposed\nto have been inherited from the Sun Goddess and his ancestors, to whom he is\naccountable.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Whenever a Japanese ship is delivered, the Captain has to recite the Shinto prayers and do some bowing before the Shinto deity. The priests look exactly like in the picture below. An altar will be there on the corner of the Navigating bridge. I have done this ceremony several times.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1WmeHOFjH9E/UH7MOnYePiI/AAAAAAAAVV0/OpCFOekq0vA/s1600/200px-Yasaka-jinja_01.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"330\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1WmeHOFjH9E/UH7MOnYePiI/AAAAAAAAVV0/OpCFOekq0vA/s400/200px-Yasaka-jinja_01.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">They perceive foreign monarchies as the creation of mere mortals,\nwhile Japan has a sacred throne, inherited from the Imperial ancestors and from\nthe gods. Therefore Japanese Imperial rule and the heavenly-created throne are\nan extension of heaven, and beyond men's powers. there is nothing on the soil\nof Japan existent independent of him. He is the sole owner of the Empire, the\nauthor of law, justice, privilege, and honor, and the symbol of the unity of\nthe Japanese nation.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0QLJN_8dGeo/UH7QO9MkTNI/AAAAAAAAVY8/fd9BwLZD5vQ/s1600/imagesnhhfdd.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-0QLJN_8dGeo/UH7QO9MkTNI/AAAAAAAAVY8/fd9BwLZD5vQ/s320/imagesnhhfdd.jpg\" width=\"207\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">He has no pope or archbishop to crown him at his\naccession. He is supreme in all temporal affairs of State as well as in all\nspiritual matters; and he is the foundation of Japanese social and civic morality.\nFrom him everything emanates; in him everything subsists.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-elfEM2OnibQ/UH6-rNQKCOI/AAAAAAAAVUw/q0gKnM7oYik/s1600/Unit731S.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"409\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-elfEM2OnibQ/UH6-rNQKCOI/AAAAAAAAVUw/q0gKnM7oYik/s400/Unit731S.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">All Japanese pupils\nbowed in the direction of the Imperial Palace, repeated by heart the long\nImperial Rescript on Education, then sang the national anthem, and waited\nbreathlessly for the question, 'What is your dearest ambition?' If one country went to war, the other two were to also declare war on the\noffending country. For FDR, this meant war with Japan would automatically put\nthe United States at war with Germany.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kAcTvBJtqdQ/UHjTS53MchI/AAAAAAAAVCM/tWlwue8BJX0/s1600/imagesmjjhtfrffgg.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"363\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kAcTvBJtqdQ/UHjTS53MchI/AAAAAAAAVCM/tWlwue8BJX0/s640/imagesmjjhtfrffgg.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">A year before the\nattack, FD Roosevelt ordered the Pacific to relocate from the US West Coast to\nHawaii. &nbsp;When its commander, Admiral\nRichardson, protested that Pearl Harbor offered inadequate protection from air\nand torpedo attack by Japanese he was arbitrarily replaced.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On October 7 1940 Navy\nIQ analyst McCollum wrote an eight-point memo for Roosevelt on how to force\nJapan into war with U.S., including a critical American oil embargo against\nJapan. FDR would follow this plan.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Japanese were severely\nprovoked into a pre-emptive strike for the sake of survival. Almost the same way Saddam Hussain was\nprovoked. On July 25, 1941, Roosevelt froze Japanese assets in the United\nStates.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dfOkJfPYiOY/UHjUme8tShI/AAAAAAAAVC8/j1hvHL4sQwA/s1600/pearl-harbor-uss-arizona.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"505\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dfOkJfPYiOY/UHjUme8tShI/AAAAAAAAVC8/j1hvHL4sQwA/s640/pearl-harbor-uss-arizona.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">US President FD\nRoosevelt was able to double check the spy information given by Bernard Baruch,\non 24th Sept 1941. This is 12 days before the attack on Pearl Harbor..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">By the summer of 1940,\nthe United States had cracked Japan's top-secret diplomatic code, nicknamed\n\"Purple\" This enabled U.S. intelligence agencies to monitor all\ndiplomatic messages to and from Tokyo.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Although several U.S.\ncommand posts having nothing to do with the Japanese, received machines for decoding \"Purple,\" Pearl Harbor\nwas never given one. &nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; There was no reason to know the EXACT location of ships\nin harbor, unless it was to attack them - it was a drop dead giveaway.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">27 January 1941, Dr.\nRicardo Shreiber, the Peruvian envoy in Tokyo told Max Bishop, third secretary\nof the US embassy that he had just learned from his intelligence sources that\nthere was a war plan involving a surprise attack on Pearl Harbor. This information\nwas sent to the State Department and Naval Intelligence and to Admiral Kimmel\nat Hawaii.<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; It was desirable to make sure\nthe Japanese be the ones to do this so that there should remain no doubt in\nanyone's mind as to who were the aggressors.\".<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On November 26th, the\nday after Roosevelt\u2019s diary entry, he received a call from Winston Churchill. A\nlarge Japanese fleet including six aircraft carriers had recently gone missing\nand Churchill said to Roosevelt in the recording \"I can assure you that\ntheir goal is the (cuts out) fleet in Hawaii, at Pearl Harbor.\"&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">This POLICY they are talking about is Rothschild\u2019s policy-- the\nJewish policy for a separate homeland .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;
