Honolulu time).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 25 Nov 1941. -\nBritish decrypted the Winds setup message sent Nov. 19. The US decoded it Nov.\n28. It was a J-19 Code message that there would be an attack and that the\nsignal would come over Radio Tokyo as a weather report - rain meaning war, east\n(Higashi) meaning USA Pearl Harbor.</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On November 25 1941, 11 days before the attack, Secretary\nof War Stimson wrote in his de-classified diary that FDR said an attack was\nlikely within days, and asked &nbsp;\"how we should maneuver them into the\nposition of firing the first shot without too much danger to ourselves. In\nspite of the risk involved, however, in letting the Japanese fire the first\nshot, we realized that in order to have the full support of the American people\nit was desirable to make sure that the Japanese be the ones to do this so that\nthere should remain no doubt in anyone's mind as to who were the\naggressors.\"<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 25 Nov 1941 the US\nNavy Department ordered all \u201cpotential WHISTLE BLOWERS \u201c the US trans-Pacific\nshipping to take the southern route. PHH 12:317 (PHH = 1946 Congressional\nReport, vol. 12, page 317) ADM Turner testified \"We sent the traffic down\nto the Torres Straight, so that the track of the Japanese task force would be\nclear of any traffic.\" PHH 4:1942<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On November 26 , 1941, 10\ndays before the attack, President FD Roosevelt was told by Bernard Baruch, to order\nboth US aircraft carriers, the Enterprise and the Lexington, out of Pearl\nHarbor ASAP. This order included stripping Pearl Harbour of 50 planes or 40\npercent of its already inadequate fighter protection. On the same day Cordell\nHull issued his provoker ultimatum demanding full Japanese withdrawal from\nIndochina and all China. U.S. Ambassador to Japan called this \"The\ndocument that touched the button that started the war.\"<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On Nov 26 1941, along\nwith the orders for the aircraft carriers&nbsp;\nthe Enterprise and the Lexington to get out of&nbsp; Pearl Harbor\u2014there was another bizarre order\n--&nbsp; stripping Pearl Harbor of 50 planes\nor 40% of its already inadequate fighter protection. In response to\nChurchill's message, FDR secretly cabled him that afternoon -\n\"Negotiations off. Services expect action within two weeks.\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On November 27, 1941 , ten\ndays before the attack on Pearl Harbor, the U.S. Navy and War Departments\nwarned \u201cNegotiations with Japan looking toward the stabilization of conditions\nin the Pacific have ceased\u2026.an aggressive move by Japan is expected within the\nnext few days.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On November 27, 1941, nine days before the attack, General George Marshall kept his own yard arm clear, and sent the\nfollowing message: \"Hostile action possible at any moment. If hostilities\ncannot, repeat CANNOT, be avoided, the United States desires that Japan commit\nthe first over act. This policy should not, repeat NOT, be construed as restricting\nyou to a course of action that might jeopardize your defense.\"</span><br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 29 Nov 1941,&nbsp; The FBI embassy tap made an intercept of an\nuncoded plain-text Japanese telephone conversation in which an Jap Embassy\nfunctionary (Kurusu) asked 'Tell me, what zero hour is. Otherwise, I won't be\nable to carry on diplomacy.' The voice from Tokyo (K. Yamamoto) said softly,\n'Well then, I will tell you. Zero hour is December 8 (Tokyo time, ie, December\n7 US time) at Pearl Harbor.' (US Navy translation 29 Nov)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\u201cThe \u2018Honolulu\nAdvertiser\u2019 front page headline on November 30, 1941 read: \u2018Japan May Strike\nover Weekend.\u2019 <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-OIuYRRdxLik/UHjO4XoiRoI/AAAAAAAAU_8/Ug43YJ6JQvA/s1600/imagesuo9p-y.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-OIuYRRdxLik/UHjO4XoiRoI/AAAAAAAAU_8/Ug43YJ6JQvA/s400/imagesuo9p-y.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">WHAT MORE DO YOU WANT ?\n&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hiLmMY3RgD8/UHjOsl1wtOI/AAAAAAAAU_0/jZusqhRYFzI/s1600/imagesjui84ervbvb.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"192\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hiLmMY3RgD8/UHjOsl1wtOI/AAAAAAAAU_0/jZusqhRYFzI/s400/imagesjui84ervbvb.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">IS THIS THE MEANING OF GETTING CAUGHT\nWITH YOUR PANTS DOWN?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 1 Dec 1941,&nbsp; FDR cut short his scheduled ten day vacation\nafter 1 day to meet with Hull and Stark. The result of this meeting was\nreported on 2 Dec. by the Washington Post: \"President Roosevelt yesterday\nassumed direct command of diplomatic and military moves relating to\nJapan.\" This politically damaging move was necessary to prevent the mutiny\nof conspirators.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Six days before the\nattack, the US intercepted a \u201cCode Purple\u201d message sent to the Japanese embassy\nin Washington, ordering them to destroy all classified documents and prepare to\nevacuate USA.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">On December 4</span><sup style=\"line-height: 150%;\">th</sup><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n1941, &nbsp;3 days before the attack, Australian\nintelligence reported to Roosevelt that the missing Japanese fleet was indeed\nmoving toward Pearl Harbor.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 4 Dec 1941 - In the\nearly hours, Ralph Briggs at the Navy's East Coast Intercept station, received\nthe \"East Winds, Rain\" message, the Winds Execute, which meant war.\nHe put it on the TWX circuit immediately and called his commander. This message\nwas deleted from the files. One of the main coverups of Pearl Harbor was to\nmake this message disappear.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">That same day the great American Hero, FD Roosevelt personally ordered the Pacific fleet moved into a compact/exposed formation\nof snug rows. &nbsp;Pearl Harbor Admiral James Richardson repeatedly objected to such\nstrategic suicide and was&nbsp; replaced for insubordination. So ,the Pearl Harbor fleet was deliberately lined up nose tip to nose tip for Japan\u2019s carpet bombing convenience. The flower of the US Navy --all the brand-new US ships and aircraft carriers were moved away, leaving only the older&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">obsolete</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;junk ships to be sacrificed.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">On 4th Dec 1941, 3 days before the attack, President FD Roosevelt, when told of the impending Japanese , with a major Japanese naval task force at sea heading towards Hawaii, directed Gen Marshall to take steps to ensure that no communications could be sent to Pearl Harbor unless cleared by Gen Marshall.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The S.S. Lurline was a passenger\nship en route from San Francisco to Hawaii . Two days before the attack the\nradio operator named Leslie Gorgan sent a communication that it was crystal\nclear that there was a large Japanese &nbsp;fleet in the Pacific. &nbsp;U.S Naval Intelligence confiscated the SS.\nLurline log days after the attack on Pearl Harbor where it was stored in a\nfederal records center in San Francisco. The log mysteriously disappeared and\nall that remains is an undated, unsigned withdrawal slip.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_kyaYrdLb_w/UHjTMpdHz-I/AAAAAAAAVCE/5dmAHjECYns/s1600/imagesgh6i0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"283\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_kyaYrdLb_w/UHjTMpdHz-I/AAAAAAAAVCE/5dmAHjECYns/s400/imagesgh6i0.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 4 Dec 1941, US\nGeneral Thorpe at Java sent four messages warning of a imminent Pear Harbor\nattack.&nbsp; FDR ordered him brusquely to\nstop sending anymore warnings.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 5th December 1941,\nFDR dictated a de-classified letter to Wendell Wilkie for the Australian Prime\nMinister, \"-- there might be an armed clash at any moment...Perhaps the\nnext four or five days will decide the matters.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 6 December 1941 at a\nWhite House dinner Roosevelt was given the first thirteen parts of a fifteen\npart decoded Japanese diplomatic declaration of war and said in front of all\npresent , \u201cGentlemen, this means War!\u201d</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Henry Stimson ( Secretary of war ) , Gen George Marshall, &nbsp;Admiral Stark , Navy Secretary Frank Knox and Harry Lloyd Hopkins ( adviser to FDR and his mouthpiece for Churchill and Stalin ) &nbsp;had spent most of the tension filled night of December\n6 , 1941 at the White House with the President FD Roosevelt.&nbsp; Everybody in White House knew something was\ncookin\u2019.&nbsp;&nbsp; You could cut the atmosphere\nthere with a&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">knife</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; All were waiting for what they knew was coming- an attack\non Pearl Harbor.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The night before the\nattack on Pearl Harbor a coded message was sent from Tokyo to the U.S. embassy\nin Washington in which Japan declared an end to diplomatic relations with the\nU.S.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Hours before the attack\non 6th Dec 1941, Gen. George C. Marshall\u2019s movements were suspicious. He left\nhis office at mid-afternoon and went for \u2013hold your breath\u2014horse riding ( if you play golf , you can be located ) in the vast Rock\nCreek Park. Then then arrived late at his Pentagon office at 11:25 Sunday\nmorning .&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Gen Marshall then read the 14-part message and the time of delivery message,\nand composed a message to army Gen. Walter Short in Hawaii, which he ordered be sent\nthrough the Signal Corps by slow commercial radio.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">A grateful Rothschild would award Gen Marshall the Nobel Peace Prize in 1953--for his role in carving out the state of Israel.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XAXbYjq7hr4/UHjOEx6ELqI/AAAAAAAAU_k/iQWSMpAVQBk/s1600/imagesbyior.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"435\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XAXbYjq7hr4/UHjOEx6ELqI/AAAAAAAAU_k/iQWSMpAVQBk/s640/imagesbyior.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Shortly after dawn on\nSunday, December 7, 1941, Japanese warplanes launched an all-out attack on\nPearl Harbor , the major U.S. military base in Hawaii. &nbsp;S</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">ix aircraft carriers of the Imperial\nJapanese Navy unleashed</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">353 dive\nbombers, torpedoes, and fighter aircraft</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CWY0wlBZEZg/UHjOVpa2smI/AAAAAAAAU_s/sk7uMErjV4A/s1600/imagesggguuuuu.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"452\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CWY0wlBZEZg/UHjOVpa2smI/AAAAAAAAU_s/sk7uMErjV4A/s640/imagesggguuuuu.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Before the day\nwas over, four battleships were sunk, three crippled, and one was run aground.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Over 300 aircraft were damaged or\ndestroyed.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">A total of 2,402 naval and\nmilitary personnel and civilians were killed, with 1178 wounded.</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Americans were stunned and outraged.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 7 December 1941, at\n1:50 P.M. Washington time. Harry Hopkins, who was the only person with FDR when\nhe received the news of the attack by telephone from Knox, wrote that FDR was\nunsurprised and expressed \"great relief.\"&nbsp; His blissfully unaware wife , the niece of\nJewish US President Theodore Roosevelt, Eleanor Roosevelt wrote about December\n7th in This I Remember p 233, that FDR became \"in a way more\nserene.\"&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Minutes after hearing\nof the attack and before any damage reports were in, US President FD Roosevelt\ncalled Lord Halifax at the British Embassy and told him \"Most of the new\nfleet and all the aircraft carriers was at sea... only old junk ships were in&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">harbor</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">.\"&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CkO5EW68utk/UHjNuMiWByI/AAAAAAAAU_c/-JPJAiiT2IU/s1600/franklin-d-roosevelt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CkO5EW68utk/UHjNuMiWByI/AAAAAAAAU_c/-JPJAiiT2IU/s320/franklin-d-roosevelt.jpg\" width=\"243\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The next day, FDR\ndelivered a stirring speech to Congress , written in advance by his speech\nwriters, in which he referred to the day of the attack as \"a date which\nwill lie in infamy.\" &nbsp;In response,\nCongress declared war, and the country closed ranks behind the president.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7BTZC7xJh1I/UHjR8VT1eLI/AAAAAAAAVBU/xrr0emcSwaI/s1600/imageskjhhfrrttyip.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"211\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7BTZC7xJh1I/UHjR8VT1eLI/AAAAAAAAVBU/xrr0emcSwaI/s320/imageskjhhfrrttyip.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The surprise vicious attack at\nPearl Harbor, coupled with other assaults throughout the western Pacific united\na bitterly divided senate and galvanized the US denizens into a thirst for\nwar and immediate cowboy posse style retribution.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hhkOhV284B0/UHjSUho-t4I/AAAAAAAAVBk/qnPfl4sR06s/s1600/imagesyj7iknbvffff.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"268\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hhkOhV284B0/UHjSUho-t4I/AAAAAAAAVBk/qnPfl4sR06s/s400/imagesyj7iknbvffff.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">FDR's attitude is best\nsummed up by co-conspirator Admiral Bloch's testimony to Congress, \"The\nJapanese only destroyed a lot of old World War 1 junk hardware. In a sense they\ndid us a favor.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">When asked about\nRoosevelt\u2019s reaction to the attack on Pearl Harbor, his administrative\nassistant, Jonathan Daniels gave the reply: \u201c The risk paid off; it was worth\nthe price\u2026\u201d <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">In 1954, Robert A.\nTheobald, Commander of Destroyers at Pearl Harbor wrote a book entitled The\nFinal Secret of Pearl Harbor in which he states it was Roosevelt that incited\nwar with Japan.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">FDR under instructions\nfrom Bernard Baruch, had sparked the largest naval buildup in U.S. history from\nthe time he took office, doubling naval personnel between 1939 and 1941 alone.</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">FDR did his charade. He\nsacked Admiral Husband Kimmel and Lt. General Walter Short stationed in Pearl\nHarbour, after the attack. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">On February 18, 1941,\nAdmiral Kimmel had written to the Chief of Naval Operations:</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\"I feel that a\nsurprise attack (submarine, air, or combined) on Pearl Harbor is a possibility,\nand we are taking immediate practical steps to minimize the damage inflicted\nand to ensure that the attacking force will pay.\"</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Admiral Kimmel and Army\nLieutenant General <b>Walter Short </b>thus became scapegoats for the diabolical\nschemes of their superiors prior to the attack on Pearl Harbor.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FB-H1cdvhLc/UHjpaOpqk4I/AAAAAAAAVEM/NcsPwCATesU/s1600/220px-Walter_C_Short.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FB-H1cdvhLc/UHjpaOpqk4I/AAAAAAAAVEM/NcsPwCATesU/s1600/220px-Walter_C_Short.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">German Jew Karl Robin\nBendetsen , carrying \"the title of Special Representative of the Secretary\nof War\" was sent by FDR on advise from Bernard Baruch to meet Major General Douglas MacArthur\nin the Philippines and also . Lieutenant General Walter C. Short (the military\ncommander in charge of Hawaiian defenses) and Rear Admiral Husband E. Kimmel\n(commander of the Pacific Fleet), leaving only days before the Pearl Harbor\nattacks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">One day after his\ninauguration to an unprecedented third term, Franklin D Roosevelt wrote to Ambassador Jew Joseph C Grew in Tokyo , explaining his belief that the war raging in Europe\nand the growing Japanese threat in the Pacific were all part of a \u201csingle world\nconflict.\u201d&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-li5VOuCIue0/UHjT9bYPn4I/AAAAAAAAVCc/qpzou2zsXRs/s1600/220px-Ambassador_Grew.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-li5VOuCIue0/UHjT9bYPn4I/AAAAAAAAVCc/qpzou2zsXRs/s1600/220px-Ambassador_Grew.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">This letter predates the\nPearl Harbor attack by nearly a year.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><i>( Secretary\u2019s Files;\nDiplomatic Correspondence; Japan, Jan.-Sept. 1941; Box 43). Document #2:&nbsp; Memorandum, Harry Dexter White to Jew Henry\nMorgenthau, Jr ( US Treasury Secretary and Rothschild US agent ) ., April 4, 1941 )<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">4 hours before the\nattack a Japanese midget submarine was spotted at 3:42am. A destroyer sank the\nsub.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">At 7:02am, a 53 minutes\nbefore the first bomb fell, radar operators at Opana Point detected the incoming\nJapanese aircraft. &nbsp;Lt. Tyler was a\nfighter pilot, in charge of the radar had only ONE day experience, and he was not\nfamiliarized . When Tyler was informed of the inbound target, Tyler famously\nsaid \"Don't worry about it,\" and they all went to have breakfast . A\n1942 court of inquiry cleared Tyler of any blame, and he went on to have an \u201cexceptional\ncareer\u201d in the Air Force\u2014how do you like that?.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Two years after the\nattack a journalist John Thomas Flynn, gave one in the eye of FDR. He&nbsp;wrote that Roosevelt himself played a hand in\nthe attack by deliberately pushing Japan into a corner. According to John T\nFlynn, he had been told in 1938 by one of Roosevelt's \"most intimate advisors\"\nthat the President would push Japan into a war so that he could fire up </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">American heavy industry\nto build battleships. This, said Flynn, was the President's way of edging out\nof the Depression, and it had worked.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Hugh Scott, a senator\nfrom Pennsylvania, said that his contacts in the Australian Government had\nwarned the administration on 6 December 9141, but had been ignored. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">No intelligence was\ngiven to Admiral Kimmel who peacefully slept oblivious to the looming storm\nthat was about to break on his Fleet. Roosevelt and his cabal of advisors,\nincluding Henry Stimson (1867-1950), the Secretary of the War, Frank Knox\n(1874-1944), the Secretary of the Navy, and Marshall, had three options. One,\nannounce to the world the approaching the Jap \u201cKido Butai\u201d&nbsp; task force obliging the Japanese to turn\nback. Two, alert Kimmel and Short to the impending danger and order them to\ntake appropriate measures, including offensive measures, which would probably,\ncause the Japanese to turn back. Three, keep Kimmel and Short in ignorance\nthereby facilitating the success of the \"surprise\" attack thereby\nprecipitating America's \"reluctant\" arrival into World War Two.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Crqj6OjfvhE/UHjQNxKQCpI/AAAAAAAAVAk/PDFQAgyPBvI/s1600/kimmel-large.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Crqj6OjfvhE/UHjQNxKQCpI/AAAAAAAAVAk/PDFQAgyPBvI/s320/kimmel-large.png\" width=\"246\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Admiral Kimmel was\nasked in an interview in 1958 for his opinion on Washington's, but especially\nRoosevelt's, treachery on that memorable day of infamy in 1941, he said: \"My\nbelief is that General Short and I were not given the information available in\nWashington and were not informed of the impending attack because it was feared\nthat action in Hawaii might deter the Japanese from making the attack. Our\npresident had repeatedly assured the American people that the United States\nwould not enter the war unless we were attacked. The Japanese attack on the\nfleet would put the United States in the war with the full support of the\nAmerican public.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-meBWTnViAwc/UHjPLKB8mTI/AAAAAAAAVAE/S2JzMlfGmTk/s1600/imagesokjhgty88.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"183\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-meBWTnViAwc/UHjPLKB8mTI/AAAAAAAAVAE/S2JzMlfGmTk/s400/imagesokjhgty88.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">It is now on record by\na confession that General George C Marshall, who went for a horse ride, just\nbefore an attack , the supreme head of the US Army ordered the cover-up of the\ntreason. \"Gentleman,\" ordained the Chief of Staff to half a dozen of\nhis trusted minions, \"this goes to the grave with us.\"<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The failure of the\nJapanese to destroy the American aircraft carriers and their fuel supply tanks\nat Pearl Harbor contributed significantly to the defeat of Japan. If the vital\nfuel storage tanks had been destroyed in either attack, the surviving American\nwarships, including the carriers Lexington and Enterprise would have been\ndeprived of fuel to operate.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DScwBONK8Gs/UHjSKT0VkiI/AAAAAAAAVBc/MklzwM2L0eU/s1600/PearlHarbor.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DScwBONK8Gs/UHjSKT0VkiI/AAAAAAAAVBc/MklzwM2L0eU/s400/PearlHarbor.jpg\" width=\"351\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Just one bullet fired upon them would have blown\nthem up and set them ablaze and NIL American oil tanker ships were bombed\neither... <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The Japanese tactical\nvictory was largely illusory. The battleships were all old and too slow, and\nthree were back in action within one month. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The powerful American\naircraft carriers Lexington and Enterprise were deliberately sent to sea when\nthe Japanese attack took place. The aircraft carrier Yorktown was on temporary\nduty in the Atlantic at this time, and was immediately ordered back to Pearl\nHarbor after the Japanese attack. The aircraft carrier Saratoga was at the San\nDiego naval base on the American West Coast when the attack occurred. <o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-g1FvSXj8UwM/UHjRSFJe87I/AAAAAAAAVBE/DvNg9PkWWhs/s1600/Enterprise.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"352\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-g1FvSXj8UwM/UHjRSFJe87I/AAAAAAAAVBE/DvNg9PkWWhs/s640/Enterprise.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The American heavy\ncruisers and submarines in Pearl Harbor were undamaged. The Pearl Harbor power\nstation,shipyard and maintenance buildings were not attacked... The torpedo\nstorage facilities were not attacked...&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JFQje3fEgBQ/UHjURHT02nI/AAAAAAAAVCs/1AMSTQZDP9g/s1600/imageshjkuytt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JFQje3fEgBQ/UHjURHT02nI/AAAAAAAAVCs/1AMSTQZDP9g/s640/imageshjkuytt.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The submarine piers and headquarters\nbuilding were not attacked... The home of the military intelligence section was\nalso not attacked...???&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">No wonder Rothschild invested in double agents and gave\nthem platinum cards to enjoy at casinos , and sow their wild oats .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On 7 December 1941, 9\nhours after the Pearl Harbour attack, Gen MacArthur's entire air force was\ncaught by surprise and wiped out in the Philippines. His reaction to the news\nof Pearl Harbor was quite unusual - he locked himself in his room all morning\nand refused to meet with his air commander General Brereton, and refused to\nattack Japanese forces on Formosa even under orders from the War Department.\nMacArthur gave three conflicting orders that ensured the planes were on the\nground most of the morning.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-P3v0sPFOv_g/UHjP9Z703mI/AAAAAAAAVAc/LjWdboGZLw4/s1600/USAmacarthur.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-P3v0sPFOv_g/UHjP9Z703mI/AAAAAAAAVAc/LjWdboGZLw4/s1600/USAmacarthur.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">MacArthur used radar tracking of the Japanese\nplanes at 140, 100, 80, 60, down to 20 miles to time his final order and ensure\nhis planes were on the ground. Strategically, the destruction of half of all US\nheavy bombers in the world was more important than naval damage in Pearl\nHarbor. It does NOT require any acuity to presume that Gen MacArthur was under\nFDR\u2019s orders to allow his forces to be destroyed..&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">This is further re-inforced\nby the fact that&nbsp; he escaped any\nreprimand, kept his command and got his fourth star and Congressional Medal of\nHonor shortly later.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Hey, how do you like that?<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-6Fd5xFdY1_w/UHjVFyU26TI/AAAAAAAAVDU/o1o6Zbm8VeM/s1600/pearl-harbor-anti-aircraft-shell.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; The kinetic energy, which may be only a fraction of the\ntotal energy, is involved in the movement or action of a body.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-l6lV3Kg-rSw/UHEVHQl_1PI/AAAAAAAAUjM/ofsTUU07NMw/s1600/8750590.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-l6lV3Kg-rSw/UHEVHQl_1PI/AAAAAAAAUjM/ofsTUU07NMw/s400/8750590.jpg\" height=\"383\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">According to\nTantra, the Kundalini, in the form of cosmic energy, is present, in everything,\neven in a particle of matter. Only a fraction of it, like the kinetic energy,\nis operative, while an unmeasured residuum is left, like the potential energy,\n\u2018coiled up\u2019 and untapped at the \u2018base root\u2019.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dQreBAVHuPE/UHEU_UrphZI/AAAAAAAAUjE/jemzrC8HLZg/s1600/imagesbrh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dQreBAVHuPE/UHEU_UrphZI/AAAAAAAAUjE/jemzrC8HLZg/s320/imagesbrh.jpg\" height=\"270\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A specific ratio between the\nactive and the total energies of the kundalini determines the present condition\nand behaviour of the bodily apparatus. A change in the ratio is necessary to\neffect a change in its present working efficiency by transforming the grosser\nbodily elements into finer. A transformation, dynamisation, and sublimination\nof the physical, mental, and vital apparatus is only possible through what is\ncalled the rousing of the Kundalini and its reorientation from \u2018downward\nfacing\u2019 to \u2018upward facing.\u2019&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7OxME06CAL8/UHEU3nmNMaI/AAAAAAAAUi8/SLm5NyZjjBw/s1600/imagesi..jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7OxME06CAL8/UHEU3nmNMaI/AAAAAAAAUi8/SLm5NyZjjBw/s200/imagesi..jpg\" height=\"200\" width=\"200\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The passage of the awakened Kundalini lies through\nthe Sushumna, which is described as the central nerve in the nervous system. A\nkind of hollow canal, the Sushumna passes through the spinal column connecting\nthe base centre (Chakra) at the bottom of the spine with the centre at the\ncerebrum. Tantra speaks of six centres (Chakras) through which Sushumna passes.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kkTGA8b8a-Y/UHEUwGjqyXI/AAAAAAAAUi0/wU_go22-bG0/s1600/imagesbfdhti.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kkTGA8b8a-Y/UHEUwGjqyXI/AAAAAAAAUi0/wU_go22-bG0/s320/imagesbfdhti.jpg\" height=\"320\" width=\"240\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the ordinary worldly person these centres (Chakras) are closed, and\nthe lotuses droop down like buds. As the Kundalini rises through the Sushumna Canal\nand touches the centres, these buds turn upward as fully opened flowers and the\naspirant obtains spiritual experiences. The goal in spiritual practice is to\nmake the Kundalini ascend from the centres, which are lower and more veiled to\nthose which are higher and more conscious..&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fnzTqIHQujc/UHEUsk5dXoI/AAAAAAAAUis/3xYs_69swCU/s1600/imagesoyyn6o.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fnzTqIHQujc/UHEUsk5dXoI/AAAAAAAAUis/3xYs_69swCU/s1600/imagesoyyn6o.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">At this sixth centre (the\ntwo-petalled white lotus located at the junction of the eyebrows) the jiva\nsheds its ego and burns the seed of duality, and its higher self rises from the\nashes of its lower self. It now dies physically, as it were, in order to be\nable to live in pure consciousness. The sixth centre is the key by which the\npower in the thousand-petalled lotus in the cerebrum, which is like the\nlimitless ocean, is switched on to the little reservoir which is the individual\nself, filling the latter and making it overflow and cease to be the little\nreservoir.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OaGuuLIxcfo/UHEUmbXUGtI/AAAAAAAAUik/P340QHEcFgE/s1600/img119-2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OaGuuLIxcfo/UHEUmbXUGtI/AAAAAAAAUik/P340QHEcFgE/s200/img119-2.jpg\" height=\"165\" width=\"200\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Finally the Kundalini rises to the lotus at the cerebrum and becomes\nunited with Shiva, or the Absolute, and the aspirant realises, in the\ntranscendental experience, his union with Siva-Sakti. The opening of the petals\nof the thousand-petalled lotus, which endows the illumined person with\nomniscience, is equivalent to the functioning of all the brain cells of a yogi\nin samadhi-- the open third eye.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Kundalini which\nexhibits pronounced psychic and trans-temporal effects is the 'channel' that\nconnects the unmanifest void, with the manifest world of subatomics, atoms,\nmolecules and cells and is the cellular expression of energy generated from the\nvacuum .</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; effect of\nstimulating an increased flow of ions upping the body\u2019s dipole and increasing\nthe EMF. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">A cell possesses two\ncharacteristics\u2014capacitance and inductance\u2014which are the elements of a tuned\ncircuit like a radio. Vishnu took his\nfifth avatar as Vamana ( the blue faced brahmin midget ) to kill our Asura king\nMahabali who was adored by the masses.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This victory of devas over asuras is the\noriginal Diwali. &nbsp;In Kerala we do NOT celebrate Diwali, for we loved our king\nMahabali, whom Vishnu killed by deceit. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8QzebZRUA00/UHCW_C-QeWI/AAAAAAAAUdc/UYyi7xszoiI/s1600/tru5u.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8QzebZRUA00/UHCW_C-QeWI/AAAAAAAAUdc/UYyi7xszoiI/s320/tru5u.jpg\" width=\"212\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Onam festival of\nKerala&nbsp; is to welcome King Mahabali every\nyear at harvest times, to reminisce good times. There were NO\nKshatriyas for Parashurama to kill. &nbsp;Basically he grabbed lands and donated it to the Namboodiris.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Kerala is a narrow\nstrip of land between the Arabian sea and the Western Ghat mountains. In those days , 6000 years ago, Kerala was an advanced society.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Broadly there were two types of people. The\nhighlanders who stayed on the mountains and the plain dwellers who lived\nbetween the sea and the mountain chain.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>The highlanders were\ncalled <span style=\"color: blue;\">Malayyars </span>(mountain top dwellers).&nbsp;</b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b><br /></b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>The plain dwellers were called\n<span style=\"color: red;\">Thirayyars</span> ( sea wave navigators ). </b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Parashurama grabbed\nlands from the Thirayyars , (called Thiyyas now ), who have all shifted to North\nKerala, from Trichur to Mangalore.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">They still continue with the matrilineal\nsystem, where women are empowered.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The lore says\nParashurama threw his axe and reclaimed the sea. The real practical meaning\ncould be that, that he used axe-power to grab the lands.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-shAmiOypDhw/UHCWa5X7pcI/AAAAAAAAUc8/FWKo4TV1A-o/s1600/e3r.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-shAmiOypDhw/UHCWa5X7pcI/AAAAAAAAUc8/FWKo4TV1A-o/s640/e3r.jpg\" width=\"468\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Even in 4000 BC when\nParshurama came here the Thirayyars traded with Palestine, Egypt , and even\nCrete. Shiva Lingams , or black&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">meteorite</span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;stones, &nbsp;have been seen at places of worship, in Cyprus and Crete.&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The patron saint of the\nKerala Thirayyars &nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">is </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rishi Therayar , the first disciple of Maharishi\nAgastya . Agastya , the greatest of the Sapt Rishis, also famous as the first\nof the Siddhas , who also founded the Kalari Payattu art of fighting.</span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; But I have seen for&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">myself</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;that they\nare very powerful forces.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Our cook was having a\nback ache, basically she was living to eat and soon developed a pot belly. It\nreached a stage that she was earning her wages doing nothing, with my wife\nslogging in the kitchen.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">So I suggested that we\nmust be practical and let go this cook and hire someone else. Or it was like\nhaving a watch dog and barking yourself.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It so transpired that\nmy wife told the broker lady to arrange for another cook. And we would continue\npaying the old cook for another 2 months, and if she still cannot heal her back\npain, then tough luck!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The new cook came, my\nwife interviewed her and we decided to keep her. She was to come after 4 days, after visiting her relatives.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then after two days the\nbroker lady came to our house and she told my wife \" I saw your old cook,\npraying at the </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>GULIKAN</b></span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> kavu.. There is NO way the new cook can come now, as the\nGulikan deity is a powerful negative force \".<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When my wife told me\nthis , I&nbsp; laughed it off. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In this present\nera, what black magic and witch craft? TEEE HEEEE!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">But my wife is very\northodox in her beliefs. She has retained the full culture of Kerala , despite\nattending school and college in Mumbai.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Today after 3 decades of marriage I can\nsay-- my wife has never eaten before me or with me. She will feed me and my\nsons children first and then eat.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This may be very difficult for a white man to\ndigest. This is our culture.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If I want to make my\nwife cry, all I need is to go to the kitchen and make a cup of tea for myself.\nAnd then whole say she will mope, like the quintessential cat, wondering what\nshe dragged in , that her master is upset.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The day the new cook\nwas supposed to come we were keeping KV ( keen&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">vigilance</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;).<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;
